@-webkit-keyframes fpFadeInDown {
  from {
    opacity: 0;
    -webkit-transform: translate3d(0, -20px, 0);
            transform: translate3d(0, -20px, 0);

@keyframes fpFadeInDown {
  from {
    opacity: 0;
    -webkit-transform: translate3d(0, -20px, 0);
            transform: translate3d(0, -20px, 0);
  }
  to {
    opacity: 1;
    -webkit-transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);
            transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);
  }
}
